<Text>Dude!! This place and whole market is a total gem and has a very welcoming atmosphere. <user>104562865931517458122< /user><Review>Overview
The new kid on the block (actually WAL Market). It's nice to see new shops opening doors in Sacramento. My experience here was good, they have been only open for 4 days so far. They offer coffee, tea and food. I'll be back!

What I ordered
‚òïÔ∏è Latte

Pros
Clean space, immediately in front of you once you enter the WAL market. The menu/offering is straightforward and simple! The latte I had was delicious and hot enough (even though I prefer hotter than most). The two employees that helped were very friendly.

Cons
No wall outlets for your computer unfortunately :(

Tips
1. Avoid the lunch time rush (if you don't want to wait), this is in the WAL Public Market.
2. The "Hand Pie" under food is only served until 1PM.
3. It's a shared space, so if you want quiet or music - bring your own headphones.<//Review>< Resp>

I've been frequenting Camellia for over a year.

The quality of coffee is great, I love the location, they'll serve you coffee in a real cup, and you can sit and relax.

The breakfast sausage sandwich is the best thing ever!  The eggs have green onions in them, the sauce is tasty and the pan is soft amd crispy on the outside. It is a full sized meal and I often split it with my wife.

Enjoy!<//Review>

1518220361032</date>
< Rate>
4</Rate>
< text>
Full disclosure: I'm friends with one of the founders but my review is still bias-free.

Cortado Review

The Pour:
Very good, tasty. They had Ethiopian beans for their espresso drinks and they use the Strauss barista blend (yay!)

Service:
Baristas were very friendly and happy to talk about their craft. One of Sacramento's premier baristas (Alfonso P) works here now. Do yourself a favor and come by when he's on bar.

Ambiance:
Clean and modern, a mix of modern and hipster. It's located in the WAL building on R Street, so kind of in the middle of Hipster Central. Next to a barber shop. You know what I'm talking about.

Conclusion:
A great new entry in Sacramento's growing roster of craft coffee shops. I've only been a couple of times, but it will no doubt be receiving it's 5th star soon, along with my other two favorite shops (Insight @ 8th St and Identity Coffee). Check it out for sure.

About Me / Review Criteria:
-I only check out / review "Third Wave"/artisanal/craft coffee shops
-Nobody gets more than 4 stars until I've gone several times
-Reviews can't be based on just a select group of baristas, they all have to be equally skilled, or at least must all have a minimum level of skill
-My star ratings are solely based on the drink, never on food, ambiance, or if the barista is emo or snobby (because that would bring down more than 50% of the shops), although I do mention those in the review
-I don't claim to be a trained coffee connoisseur
-My reviews are generally based on gibraltar/cortados (or cappuccinos), not espresso or drip/pourover coffee<//text>

<date>1441821220327<//date><Rate>4< /Rate>< Text>
I was sad to find out that Chilaberries was gone, but Aldo is a great replacement for this strip mall.

I ordered the al-Dough with Nutella gelato and strawberries.  They put those ingredients in a bun, and seal it in a waffle-esque iron.  It tasted like a funnel cake especially with the addition of powdered sugar.  It can be shared with two people because it's quite filling.  The also have custards and Italian ices.

The decor has a diner feel, and it was pretty clean.  I will probably come back again when I'm craving ice cream.<//Text>

< review>
Absolutely the best storage facility that I have ever rented from.  Staff is friendly, professional and  understanding.  The rules are common sense and reasonable. The facility itself is new, climate controlled,  well lit and all units are inside. The elevators are big and the carts are available the same hours as the gate. They also have 8 to 10?carts so usually they are available without having to wait and they do not require you to leave your keys or driver's license to use the carts. The unload is area is well lit and the lanes are long and wide so unloading is easy.
Martin is absolutely the best,  professional  and empathetic.  If you have any issues, he will try to work with you to find a solution.  The only thing that would make it more perfect would be extending the gate hours,  as it is,  the gate hours of 6am to 8pm are longer than most storage facilities in this area. They also have gate access on holidays. The office may be gone, but you still have access to your unit.
One last thing  to mention, the price for all of these great features is co.peower than other facilities</review>

< review>
Moving is easy and fun, said no one ever. We are 100% in that majority camp. With that said, Magali from StorQuest-Anaheim/Walnut was the highlight of our entire moving process.

I would go out on a limb to say that our experience with finding a new home, and subsequently moving, during a global pandemic was far from conventional. We were moving from DTLA to Anaheim and in the time of Covid, we were glad to make the normally 50-60 minute drive in half the time. Naturally, our luck ran out the weekend of our move when SoCal's economies reopened and it seemed like every car in LA/OC were on the streets and freeways at the same time. Being in bumper-to-bumper traffic usually sucks, but is exacerbated when driving a 15' U-Haul truck.

So we crawled to Anaheim, with me frantically on the phone with Magali half an hour before the office closed for us to rent our storage unit. She and I exchanged phone calls 3 times, with her on the other line being ever-so-patient, empathetic of the situation and willing to help the entire time. Although the storage unit was about to close, she was on the phone with her manager to try and accommodate us. Luckily, the manager was understanding and flexible, and allowed Magali to service us after working hours. Over the phone, she jumpstarted our application process so that all we had to do when we got to the office was pay and sign our lease. We realize that this is absolutely an exception, but in an unprecedented time, we all are experiencing our share of firsts.

When we got into the parking lot, I jumped out of the truck and ran into the office, where Magali was waiting for me. She was a sweetheart, and even more personable in person. 10 minutes later, we were starting to load up our storage unit.

The storage facility is new, clean and well-maintained, as was our unit. Access to the facility is open until 8PM (for those on the autopay plan), and when the gate closes. Our experience at StorQuest has been exceptional and exceeded our expectations, thanks to Magali! :)<//review>

Great facility & extremely clean. I had an issue with getting my hours extended since I was selling some of my items with someone on Craigslist. The buyer was mot sure when her husband could come and we were both pressed for time to leave. There was only an early or night extension to choose from. Luckily, Pati, the representative there, saw the frustration on our faces and gladly gave the extension for both! She helped us out a lot and included it for 2 days as well.  Unbeknownst to them though, the code the next morning did not work, fortunately, their phone # worked and after only a few automated questions, I got in contact with a live rep. They assisted me with the error, quickly gave me a new number and the problem was solved!

Although the service at the actual location and the lady over the phone were great... the system online for choosing a rate is a bait & switch. When I initially called and spoke with a sales rep, I was given a ‚Äúfinal price‚Äù quote of $45. I had made sure that was all it was since I had already priced out other places and they person over the phone confirmed it was. Well long behold, it was not. After taxes&fees it was $90!
